 The renowned historian of the country, Professor Bipin Chandra, died at his home in Gurgaon on Saturday morning
 vah 86 varsh ke the
 Bipin Chandra, who was the chief historian of the history of modern India, breathed his last at 6 in the morning
 unke shishy evam jawaharal laal nehru vishvavidhyalay ke acadmic staff college ke associat professor dow
 Rakesh Butbyal gave this information
 dow
 Butbayal described Bipin Chandra as a great historian, saying that he had an important contribution in the history of modern India
 unhone itihaas or rashtrawaad ko ek nayaa mode diya

 vipaksh kaa aarope he ki barish nahin hone se sookhe kii sthiti utpann ho gai he, lekin sarkaar kii usase nipatane kii koi taiyaari nahin he
 Leader of Opposition in Lok Sabha Sushma Swaraj said, the country is facing a big economic crisis
 vishwa main bhartiya arthvyavastha kii reating ghataae jane, rupee kaa avamulyan hone or inaki vajah se utpann samasyaon par ham sansad main gambhir charchaa or sarkaar ke eemaandaar jawaab kii maang karenge
 Sushma Swaraj said that apart from this, her party would like clarification about the government's intention to allow FDI in retail
 sarkaar se unhone maang kii ki is mudde par yaa to vah charchaa karaae athwa sadan main aashwaasan de ki khudara kshetra main pratyaksh videshi nivesh ko anumati nahin di jaaegi
 With Pranab Mukherjee becoming President, he will now be replaced by Sushil Kumar Shinde as Leader of the House in the Lok Sabha
 sipiem ke gurudas dasgupta ne kaha, sansad ke is satr main hamaari pehali praathamikta arthvyavastha kii sankat par charchaa karana hogi, kyonki sarkaar is sachaai par pardaa daalane ko prayasarat he
 Accusing the government of not taking a clean stand in the FDI case, he said, there is no 'dancing doll' of the Parliament government
 use vipaksh kii maangon ko gambhirtha se lenaa chahie
 upa's constituent Trinamool Congress also warned the government to desist from pursuing anti-people policies like FDI and pension bill
 7 sitambar tak chalane vaale monsoon satr main pune visphot, assam ke jaateey dange, rail durghatnaon, bijli grid ke thap hone, amarnath yatra main badi sankhya main shraddhaluon ke nidhan or maaruti sanyatra main hinsa jaise vishyon par bhi vipaksh sarkaar ko joardaar dhang se gherne kaa prayaas karegaa
 The comments sansadeey kaary mantri pawan kumaar bansal ne bataaya ki monsoon satr main 31 vidheyak vichaar ke liye rakhe jaaenge, lekin lokapal vidheyak par abhi anischitata bani hui he
 The main bills listed for this session include the Women's Reservation Bill, the Forward Contracting Bill and the Whistle Blower Bill
 pichley 42 saal se lambit bahucharchit lokapal vidheyak ke is satr main paarit hone kii sambhaavna nahin he
 Bansal said that the bill has not been listed for this session as it has not been completed in the Select Committee yet
 is vidheyak ko loksabhaa se manjuuri mil chuki he, lekin rajyasabha se iskaa paarit hona abhi baaki he
 To make the situation normal, Speaker Meira Kumar asked Advani to withdraw his remarks, which he accepted
 aisa karte hue unhone spashtikaran diya ki unki tippanee upie-2 sarkaar ke bare main nahin, balki upie-1 sarkaar ke samay vishwasamat ke dauraan hue ghatnakram ke sandarbh main thi
 Advani made the above remarks at about 12 o'clock after the Question Hour, starting a discussion on the adjournment motion on the incidents of recent ethnic violence in Assam
 sadan ke nae netaa susheel kumaar scindia ne adwani kii tippanee par sakht aapatti jataate hue kaha ki vah ek varisht netaa hai or ham unka sammaan karte hai, lekin unhone apni tippanee ke dwaara puure chunaav ko avaidh qaraar de diya he, jo ham sab ke liye apmaan kii baat he
 They should take back their words
 sansadeey kaary mantri pawan kumaar bansal ne vyavastha kaa prashn uthaate hue kaha ki jis vishay par kaarysthgan prastaav diya jaataa he, keval usee par baat rakhe jane kii anumati rahati he, lekin adwani duusare vishay ko uthaa rahe hai
 Amid the ongoing uproar by the ruling and opposition members, Speaker Meira Kumar adjourned the house for lunch at 1 pm
 sansad ke monsoon satr ke pehle hi din loksabhaa main assam hinsa ke mudde par or rajyasabha main vipaksh or sarkaar ko baahar se samarthan de rahi basapa ke sadasyon ke vibhinn muddon par hangaame ke kaaran kaarywahi 12 baarah baje tak sthagit kar di gai
 Earlier, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh said that the government is ready to hold debate on any subject as per the rules and conventions of the Parliament and also hoped that the opposition would extend all possible cooperation in carrying out the official work in both the Houses
 sansad kii imaarat ke bheetar pravesh karne se pehle samvaadadaataaon se baat karte hue unhone kaha, hamaari sarkaar kisi bhi mudde par sansad ke niyamon or paramparaon ke anuroop bahes karaane ke liye taiyaar he
 Asked about the BJP bringing an adjournment motion on the issue of ethnic violence in Assam, Singh said, "we consider Parliament as a forum for debate
" unhone kaha ki assam kii hinsa ke bare main unke bayaan kaa faisla is baat par nirbhar karegaa ki sansad main kya kuch hota he
 Singh said that he hoped that all parties would cooperate with the government in the smooth functioning of the two houses during the monsoon session
 is satr ke dauraan sarkaar sansad main kareeb 31 bill pesh karegi, haalanki lokapal bill abhi list main nahin he
 According to the strategists of the government, after the introduction of the bill from the Select Committee, it can be introduced in the Rajya Sabha

 sattapaksh or vipaksh ke sadasyon kii ore se kaaphi der se jari hangaame ke bich adhyaksh mira kumaar ne sadan kii kaarywahi 1 baje bhojanavkaash ke liye sthagit kar di
 On the very first day of the monsoon session of Parliament, the proceedings were adjourned till 12 noon due to uproar over the issue of Assam violence in the Lok Sabha and various issues in the Rajya Sabha by the opposition and members of the BSP supporting the government from outside
 isse pehle, pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne kaha ki sarkaar sansad ke niyamon or paramparaon ke anusaar kisi bhi vishay par bahes karaane ke liye taiyaar he or saath hi ummid jataai ki vipaksh donon sadanon main sarkari kaamkaaj ko puraa karne main harsambhav sahyog degaa
 Speaking to reporters before entering the Parliament building, he said, "our government is ready to debate any issue in accordance with the rules and traditions of Parliament
" assam main jaateey hinsa ke maamle ko lekar bijepi kii ore se kaarysthgan prastaav laae ke bare main puche jane par singh ne kaha, ham sansad ko bahes kaa manch maanate hai
 He said that the decision of his statement about the violence in Assam will depend on what happens in Parliament
 singh ne kaha ki unhen ummid he ki sabhi dal monsoon satr ke dauraan donon sadanon ke kaamkaaj ko sahaj dhang se chalaane main sarkaar kaa sahyog karenge
 During this session, the government will introduce about 31 bills in Parliament, although the Lokpal bill is not yet in the list
 sarkaar ke ranneetikaron kii maane to select cameti se bill ke aane ke baad use rajyasabha main pesh kiya ja saktaa he
 Apart from this, the opposition will also try to surround the government on alleged scams like spectrum, coal block allocation and aircel-maxis deal
 tamilnadu express train main lagi aag sahit pichley kuch dinon main badhati rail durghatnaon ke maamalon ko uthaakar sarkaar kii dukhati rag ko dabaane kaa bhi prayaas hoga
 The Ministry of Railways is with the Trinamool Congress led by Mamta Banerjee, which is an ally of the Congress
 is saal desh ke adhiktar hisse main monsoon kii kami kaa vishay bhi sansad main jor-shor se uthegaa
 The opposition alleges that drought has arisen due to no rain, but the government is not prepared to deal with it
 loksabhaa main vipaksh kii netaa sushamaa swaraj ne kaha, desh bade aarthik sankat kaa saamana kar rahaa he
 We will demand a serious discussion in Parliament and an honest answer to the government on the downgrade of the Indian economy in the world, the devaluation of the rupee and the problems arising out of them
 sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki iske alaava khudara kshetra main pratyaksh videshi nivesh kii anumati die jane kii sarkaar kii manshaa ke bare main unki party spashtikaran chaahegi
 He demanded from the government that either he should discuss this issue or give assurance in the House that FDI in retail will not be allowed
 pranab mukherjee ke raashtrapati ban jane se loksabhaa main ab unki jagah susheel kumaar scindia sadan ke netaa ke rup main dikhenge
 Gurudas Dasgupta of CPM said, "our first priority in this session of Parliament will be to discuss the crisis of the economy, because the government is trying to cover this truth
" epadiai maamle main sarkaar par saaf rukh nahin apnaane kaa aarope lagaate hue unhone kaha, sansad sarkaar kii koi 'naachati gudiya' nahin he
 He should take the opposition's demands seriously
 upie ke ghatak dal trinmul congress ne bhi sarkaar ko chetavanee di ki vah epadiai or pension vidheyak jaisi jan-virdohi nitiyon ko aage badhaane se baj aae
 Opposition also strongly surrounds the government on topics such as Pune blast, Assam riots, rail accidents, power grid collapse, large number of pilgrims dying in Amarnath Yatra and violence at Maruti plant in the monsoon session lasting till 7 September Will try tippaniyan Parliamentary Affairs Minister Pawan Kumar Bansal said that 31 bills will be put up for consideration in the monsoon session, but there is still uncertainty over the Lokpal bill
 is satr ke liye soochibaddh mukhya vidheyakon main mahila aarakshan vidheyak, vaayada anubandhan vidheyak or visal bloir vidheyak shaamil hai
 The much-discussed Lokpal Bill, which has been pending for the last 42 years, is unlikely to be passed in this session
 bansal ne kaha ki is vidheyak kii abhi pravar samiti main samiksha puri nahin ho paane ke kaaran ise is satr ke liye abhi soochibaddh nahin kiya gaya he

 - Narendra Modi (@narendramodi) January 29, 2019 Political journey has been a historic contribution of former Defense Minister George Fernandes in Indian politics, whether it is the big decisions taken in defense sector or the issue of raising his voice during Emergency
 , George Fernandes always took the lead
 purv raksha mantri jorge furnandis kii aguwai main 1974 main hui railway hadtaal ko sabase badi hadtaal ke rup main dekha jaataa he
